app.post("/nakshatra", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const nakshatra = new Nakshatra(req.body);
    await nakshatra.save();
    res.status(201).json({ message: "Nakshatra data saved successfully", data: nakshatra });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Error saving Nakshatra data", details: error.message });
  }
});
